  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ab817e55-3002-4908-9c69-0024b251dfff'
      });

  <span id="freeText11250649828249422324" style="display:none"><b>Four young ladies at the side of the ballroom make a pact to help each other find husbands...no matter what it takes...</b><br /><br />Proud and beautiful Annabelle Peyton could have her pick of suitors—if only she had a dowry. Her family is on the brink of disaster, and the only way Annabelle can save them is to marry a wealthy man. Unfortunately her most persistent admirer is the brash Simon Hunt, a handsome and ambitious entrepreneur who wants her as his mistress.<br /><br />Annabelle is determined to resist Simon's wicked propositions, but she can't deny her attraction to the boldly seductive rogue, any more than he can resist the challenge she presents. As they try to outmaneuver each other, they find themselves surrendering to a love more powerful than they could have ever imagined. But fate may have other plans—and it will take all of Annabelle's courage to face a peril that could destroy everything she holds dear.<p></p></span>

<a href="/questions/1432747-i-really-wanted-to-like-this-book-but-i"><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I really wanted to like this book but I couldn't because only due to a plot point where Simon changes his mind about her being his mistress. Things like that did not happen in regency England. A man was clear about who could be a wife or a mistress. His explanation did not convince me. Can anyone help clear this up ? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I've just re-read this book and feel that he always wanted her, anyway he could get her - he fell in love with her long before she did with him. I thi<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I've just re-read this book and feel that he always wanted her, anyway he could get her - he fell in love with her long before she did with him. I think the heroine just assumed that he wanted her as a mistress, because of their class differences. And so she was shocked when he offered to marry her because of that assumption. Perhaps I missed something?<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1350157055" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511556834p2/28967089.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1350157055?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession">Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=own-book">own-book</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1350157055" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7850170249186936422"><b>4.5 I love you Dammit Stars</b><br/><br/><b>***********Spoilers**********</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9820387_zpsxcmwcc6z.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484467585ra/21721127.gif' alt=' photo 9820387_zpsxcmwcc6z.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“You…you mustn’t stare at me like that.” Soft as the murmur was, he caught it. “With you here, nothing else is worth looking at.” -Annabelle and Simon</b><br/><br/>I love Lisa Kleypas! Now a little while back I bought the whole Hathaways series for 4.00 and it was my first taste of Lisa Kleypas. I fell madly in love with all the Hathaways and when I finished that series I went to goodreads to find more books by LK to read. That was when I found out t</span>
  <span id="freeText7850170249186936422" style="display:none"><b>4.5 I love you Dammit Stars</b><br><br><b>***********Spoilers**********</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9820387_zpsxcmwcc6z.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484467585ra/21721127.gif" alt=" photo 9820387_zpsxcmwcc6z.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“You…you mustn’t stare at me like that.” Soft as the murmur was, he caught it. “With you here, nothing else is worth looking at.” -Annabelle and Simon</b><br><br>I love Lisa Kleypas! Now a little while back I bought the whole Hathaways series for 4.00 and it was my first taste of Lisa Kleypas. I fell madly in love with all the Hathaways and when I finished that series I went to goodreads to find more books by LK to read. That was when I found out that The Wallflower series is connected to the Hathaway series and was suppose to be read first. Oops. Of course I went out to every book store I know and found the whole Wallflowers series for a 1.00 each. It was such a good buy! I enjoyed Secrets Of A Summer Night!!! It was everything I love about LK's books. Annabelle and Simon's story was so very sweet. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_lfbx34BQ101qgq107o1_500_large_zpszpk1e8sf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484467585ra/21721128.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lfbx34BQ101qgq107o1_500_large_zpszpk1e8sf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Let me spoil you,” he whispered. “Let me take care of you. You’ve never had anyone to lean on, have you? I’ve got strong shoulders, Annabelle.”-Simon</b><br><br><br>Annabelle took me a bit to warm up to. At first I wanted to shake Annabelle because she was so snobby and full of self importance. I hated the way she looked down at Simon like he wasn't good enough for her just because he wasn't peer. But slowly she realized that she was a prejudice snob and that Simon was great. And as she grew as a person she grew on me as well. I ended up loving her. She turned out to be a brave, sweet, and loyal. Simon omg Simon!!!! He was amazing and made the book for me. I love a man that knows what he wants and goes for it. I got that in spades with Simon. He seen Annabelle and he set out to have her. Period! He went after her like a lion going for a gazelle. Simon was sexy, sweet, honest to the point of rude at times, possessive, and confident. I loved how he slowly broke down all Annabelle's walls and worked his way into her heart. He could see the wonderful person she was underneath. I also loved that he seen her worth when all the other men seen a broke woman they could take a vantage of. But the thing that melted my heart was that Simon thought she was sleeping with a man for money and didn't care that she wasn't a virgin he still wanted to marry her and take care of her. Of course she was a virgin he was wrong but the point was it didn't matter to him. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/hes-just-so-wonderful_zps0u52aw9y.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484467585ra/21721129.gif" alt=" photo hes-just-so-wonderful_zps0u52aw9y.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I love you, dammit.” She brushed her lips teasingly against his. “How much?” He made a slight sound, as if the soft kiss had affected him intensely. “Without limit. Beyond forever.” “I love you more,”-Simon and Annabelle</b><br><br>Simon and Annabelle's relationship was a slow burn since at first she would snub him. But they had serious passion. I felt they had a great build up to a sweet love. It felt real. Simon was so sweet to Annabelle after they were married. He really took care of her and her family. And Annabelle fell hard for her husband. They both had a playful side that was cute. One of my favorite things about this book was the friendship between Annabelle and her fellow Wallflowers Lillian, Daisy, and Evie. They were a funny band of misfits hell bent on finding husbands and helping each other in any way they could. My favorite of the group was Lillian. She was so outspoken and foul mouthed. I loved how her and Earl Westcliff (Marcus) butted heads and took a dislike to each other. There was some major passion burning under all that hate and I can't wait to read their book! This was a sweet, romantic read and I loved it! I only took off a 1/2 star for Annabelle's snobby attitude because I wish she would have changed sooner. Other than that it was perfect! These 2 quotes just sums it up so nicely!! They are my favorite quotes of the whole book!<br><br><b>“I realized something,” she said huskily, “when I was standing outside the foundry, watching it burn and knowing you were inside.” She swallowed hard against the thickness in her throat. “I would rather have died in your arms, Simon, than face a lifetime without you. All those endless years… all those winters, summers… a hundred seasons of wanting you and never having you. Growing old, while you stayed eternally young in my memories.” She bit her lip and shook her head, while her eyes flooded. “I was wrong when I told you that I didn’t know where I belonged. I do. With you, Simon. Nothing matters except being with you. You’re stuck with me forever, and I’ll never listen when you tell me to go.” -Annabelle<br><br><br>“My God, I can’t stand this! I can’t let you go out every day, fearing every minute that something might happen to you, knowing that every ounce of sanity I’ve got left is hinged on your well-being. I can’t feel this way…it’s too strong…oh, hell. I’ll turn into a raving lunatic. I’ll never be of use to anyone again. If I could just reduce it somehow…love you only half this much…I might be able to live with it.”-Simon</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7850170249186936422" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_36563950" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/36563950" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/36563950?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Victorian Romance With Self-Made Heroes</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=knight-in-tarnished-armor">knight-in-tarnished-armor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-in-pursuit">hero-in-pursuit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=self-made-hero">self-made-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=marriage">marriage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer36563950&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer36563950" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer797975166838388953">Gosh, what a standout start to the Wallflowers series. Simon is a definite hero in pursuit, one of my favorite types. He saw Annabelle and he had to have her. He wasn't always upstanding in the things he said or did, or his motivations. But it didn't help that Annabelle's inbred snobbery caused her to look down at him. Simon is a self-made man. He is very wealthy and his wealth has opened doors for him socially (just barely). The fact that he is a business associate (and friend of Lord Westcliff</span>
  <span id="freeText797975166838388953" style="display:none">Gosh, what a standout start to the Wallflowers series. Simon is a definite hero in pursuit, one of my favorite types. He saw Annabelle and he had to have her. He wasn't always upstanding in the things he said or did, or his motivations. But it didn't help that Annabelle's inbred snobbery caused her to look down at him. Simon is a self-made man. He is very wealthy and his wealth has opened doors for him socially (just barely). The fact that he is a business associate (and friend of Lord Westcliff) does help him to get into this society that he really doesn't care about, except that it allows him to be close to the object of his desire, Annabelle Peyton. But Annabelle has been raised from the cradle to seek a marriage with a gentleman at the least, and a titled one, if entirely possible. Plus I think she is a little intimidated at how intensely Simon seems to want her, and how he is such a strong, vital man (not what she would consider an English gentleman at all). The first half of this book is a bit of a cat and mouse chase, as Simon spends his time hunting down the wary Annabelle. <br><br>Can I just say I adored Simon? He is just delicious to me. I love a strong, independent, self-made hero, who doesn't spend his time worrying about what others think. Annabelle came off as kind of mercenary. Yet I found I could not dislike her. She was in desperate straits. I could see why she was so fixated on making a good match. Yet at the same time, I wanted to yell at her, "Hey, Simon is loaded. He's hot. He wants you. Marry him." Let's be honest. I would have been throwing myself at Simon. He's one of my all time favorite LK heroes (top three). Yes I know he's got some ungentlemanly intentions towards Annabelle, but I felt that he would take her any way he could get her. <br><br>He shows his love and devotion in many ways. I love the scene when he cares for Annabelle when she gets snakebitten. He totally could have taken advantage of her, but he didn't. And things are getting where she doesn't have the luxury to wait for an honorable offer. Yet he ended up offering marriage, after all. Because he loved her to the depths of his soul. Sigh! And what a good husband he is. <br><br>Now after their marriage, I felt some frustration towards Annabelle for her snobbery against Simon's family. I can understand culture shock, but she was married to Simon, and her life had changed permanently. I didn't really see her setting her mind on the fact that she was now a middle class businessman's wife to the degree that I hoped for. She liked the trappings of being a rich man's wife, but didn't like to think about how he made his money or his origins. It took that potentially tragic event for her to snap out of her 'old' thinking mode and see what a wonderful love and life she could have with Simon.<br><br>I didn't care for Westcliff that much at first. But when Westcliff tells her off, I started to warm to him. Before that, he was rather cold. But you could see he disliked Annabelle because he didn't really think she deserved Simon. To be frank, I was somewhat agreeing with him. I felt I could like this cold, aristocratic man when he risked his life to save Simon who was socially beneath him and was protective about him against a 'fortune-hunting adventuress,' which was how he saw Annabelle. I felt that Westcliff knew Annabelle pretty well, because in some ways they were of the same mindset and were having to open their minds to the fact that the Old England was changing as the century wound to a close. I liked that they became a united front in their mutual caring for Simon. <br><br>It may sound as if I am being harsh about Annabelle. I really like her despite her snobby tendencies. She is a very sweet, kind person, and was good to the other Wallflowers. She has a good sense of humor and was a good daughter. I just tend to be very protective about my favorite heroes. I want their heroine to be completely in love with them, because my favorite heroes are the type who are 110% in love with their heroine. They should be loved to the same intensity. I hate when the feeling is unequal in a romance. I was glad that Annabelle finally came around, although I wished it was a little bit sooner.<br><br>This is my second favorite Wallflower (after Devil in Winter) because I loved the fact that Simon was a man who set himself on a course, and never gave up. That course was winning his heroine, Annabelle. I loved the friendship between the four wallflowers, Annabelle, Lillian, Daisy, and my favorite, sweet Evie. You get the impression that the friendship they form will stand the test of time. And you hope they will all meet and marry men worthy of them. Also I loved the late Victorian setting, and how rich the descriptions of this time and the people are in this story. Secrets of a Summer Night is definitely one of my all time favorite Lisa Kleypas novels.<br><br>Actors I would cast as Simon and Annabelle: Christian Bale and Kate Beckinsale.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><span>[image error]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="797975166838388953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1641543674?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alp" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alp" href="/user/show/26653561-alp">Alp</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1641543674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4944988517947347723">What a wonderful story!<br/><br/>This was another gem from one of my favorite authors. As always, Lisa Kleypas never ever fails me. Secrets of A Summer Night had me hooked from the very start, enraptured me in a way that I never imagined, and I found myself having a hard time putting it down.<br/><br/>I loved Simon Hunt! He’s strong, smart, swoon-worthy, and sweet. Yet he could be a bad boy at times. No matter how rich he is, the peers have never accepted him as one of themselves. For the fact that he was born a co</span>
  <span id="freeText4944988517947347723" style="display:none">What a wonderful story!<br /><br />This was another gem from one of my favorite authors. As always, Lisa Kleypas never ever fails me. Secrets of A Summer Night had me hooked from the very start, enraptured me in a way that I never imagined, and I found myself having a hard time putting it down.<br /><br />I loved Simon Hunt! He’s strong, smart, swoon-worthy, and sweet. Yet he could be a bad boy at times. No matter how rich he is, the peers have never accepted him as one of themselves. For the fact that he was born a commoner, a butcher’s son, he knows exactly who he is and never pretends to be someone he’s not. He was attracted to Annabelle since the first time he laid eyes on her and he couldn’t get her out of his mind. Two years later, Annabelle had remained unwed and Simon was more than ready to claim her as his own.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’ve wanted you since the first moment I saw you standing outside that panorama, digging for coins in your purse. I couldn’t take my eyes from you. I could hardly believe you were real.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Annabelle Peyton and her family were in desperate straits. Marrying a wealthy nobleman was the only way for her to save her mother and her brother. I was surprised at how much I enjoyed her character. She’s strong-willed, independent, and smart. Despite her lack of dowry, the way she ignored Simon’s offer was a reflection of the value she placed on herself.<br /><br />It was so sweet seeing Simon taking care of Annabelle in a time of need. And it was so lovely that their feelings grew stronger and deeper for each other with each moment they shared together. I loved the sizzling chemistry between them and how they couldn’t keep their hands off each other and certainly, the way they kissed. **Melt** Not to mention their steamy hot and passionate sexy times.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I have no self-control where you’re concerned. Every minute that I’m not with you, all I can think about is being inside you. I hate everything that keeps you separate from me.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />This was a very well-written and heartwarming story with an engaging plot, adorable characters, and breathtakingly beautiful romance. It was hilarious, refreshing, and touching all at the same time. Simon and Annabelle’s love story made my heart swell and the ending brought tears to my eyes. The banter between the 4 wallflowers was witty and true to life.<br /><br />I don’t want to say much more because this is a book you should read it for yourself.<br /><br />By the way, this was a very good historical romance story. I was overjoyed that I decided to pick up this one. Loved it!<br /><br /><br />----------------------------------------<br /><br /><br /><b>**Thanks for the buddy read, lovely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1578257071?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Ally</a>.</b></span>

<div id="review_21987630" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/21987630" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/21987630?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone who loves historicals</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2010_reads">2010_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer21987630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11867810790062310381">First of all, a big fat boot in the rear (to me) for letting this gem languish in the TBR for so long! Why am I so stubborn? So I have drifted away from historicals, but c'mon, this is Kleypas--I should've known better! I've loved so many of her books, and her heroes are some of my all time favorite romance heroes (Zachary Bronson, Jack Devlin, Derek Craven)--now I can add one more to the list--the deliciously sexy Simon Hunt (be still my heart)! I <i>loved</i> this guy! Talk about swoon-worthy! I'm te</span>
  <span id="freeText11867810790062310381" style="display:none">First of all, a big fat boot in the rear (to me) for letting this gem languish in the TBR for so long! Why am I so stubborn? So I have drifted away from historicals, but c'mon, this is Kleypas--I should've known better! I've loved so many of her books, and her heroes are some of my all time favorite romance heroes (Zachary Bronson, Jack Devlin, Derek Craven)--now I can add one more to the list--the deliciously sexy Simon Hunt (be still my heart)! I <i>loved</i> this guy! Talk about swoon-worthy! I'm telling you, there was a time or two that I was wondering if Annabelle Peyton had rocks for brains, rebuffing Mr. Hunt--who wants to marry a 'peer' when you can have Simon (even if he was not the 'marrying type')?<br><br>I know Annabelle had her mind set on marrying a peer to get out of a horrible financial predicament, and Simon (son of a working class butcher) was anything but. But there was this sizzling attraction, even though she didn't want there to be. This book was just <i>filled</i> with sexual tension, and had me on the edge, just wondering when (and how) Annabelle was going to give in to the temptation that was Simon. So he wasn't a peer, he wasn't the marrying kind, he wasn't in her social class (even though he was filthy rich due to hard work), he wasn't the physical ideal (he was big and brawny and rough looking), and she thought of him as ill-bred...but she couldn't deny the connection that they had. I loved the verbal sparring that they did, loved the whole Scarlett/Rhett vibe, loved how she tried to put him in his place and loved how he came back for more, and wouldn't be denied. He wanted Annabelle and he was going to have her!<br><br>What else did I love? Her relationship with the other "Wallflowers". The scenes with the bold Americans Lillian and Daisy Bowman, and the shy, stuttering Evie Jenner were some of my favorite (non-Simon) scenes in the book. It was so funny how they plotted to snag an appropriate husband for Annabelle (not that I approved of their methods--but their conversations were often hilarious)! And their game of 'Rounders' (which sounds like baseball) where they played in their drawers, only to be seen by Lord Westcliff and Simon? So well written--loved the defiance shown by Annabelle and Lillian!<br><br>*******spoilers********<br>But my favorite scenes were the ones involving Annabelle and Simon. The extended chess game (*sigh*), the tending to Annabelle after the snake bite (*sigh*), the purchase of the boots (*sigh*), and the <i>honeymoon</i> (Yowza!)...and the bit of suspense at the end, and the declaration(s) of love? P-e-r-f-e-c-t-i-o-n.<br><br>Oh, I could go on and on, but I'm <i>dying</i> to start "It Happened One Autumn"--I want to see the stuffy Lord Westcliff redeem himself in my eyes. For this first book of <b>The Wallflowers</b> series--5 big stars!<br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=joemanganiello-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311061i/688364.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>My idea for Simon</span>
  <a data-text-id="11867810790062310381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2114354003" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2114354003" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2114354003?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6587379-secrets-of-a-summer-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=guilty-pleasure-read">guilty-pleasure-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2114354003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10323647272405334409"><b> 4 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Having regrets is the only sign that you’ve done anything interesting with your life.” </i> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504638707ra/23796046.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The first book in the Wallflower series, Secrets of a Summer Night is about Annabelle, a beautiful woman searching for a husband, but her family’s financial troubles prevent this. No man wants to marry a woman with no dowry, but Annabelle must marry soon to prevent her family from being put out on the streets.<br/><br/>Annabelle’s only luck seems to be with Simon Hunt, a man not of the nobility, but one wh</span>
  <span id="freeText10323647272405334409" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Having regrets is the only sign that you’ve done anything interesting with your life.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504638707ra/23796046.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first book in the Wallflower series, Secrets of a Summer Night is about Annabelle, a beautiful woman searching for a husband, but her family’s financial troubles prevent this. No man wants to marry a woman with no dowry, but Annabelle must marry soon to prevent her family from being put out on the streets.<br><br>Annabelle’s only luck seems to be with Simon Hunt, a man not of the nobility, but one who mad a great deal of money is business. He’s unrefined, blunt and even worse, he does not want Annabelle for his wife but as his mistress. <br><br>Befriending three other wallflowers at a ball, they make a pact to help get every single one of them married, and first up is Annabelle as this is her last season to find a husband. They concoct a plan, and hopefully they’re mischievous ways will work!<br><br><br><b> <i> “I spent most of my youth hauling sides of beef and pork to my father's shop. Carrying you is far more enjoyable."<br><br>"How sweet," Annabelle mumbled sickly, her eyes closed. "Every woman dreams of being told that she's preferable to a dead cow.” </i> </b><br><br>Historical romance is not my go to genre, but it’s so fun to dabble in from time to time. Lisa Kleypas is an author I really click with because I don’t end up rolling my eyes at the language or actions of the characters. She does her research really well, and is able to make a smooth transition into whatever time period she places her books in.<br><br>I also normally don’t like Cinderella stories, and the rags to riches trope. But I loved Annabelle as a character, she was strong but had morals and pride. Her relationship with Hunt was a hate to love kind of story where over time the two get to know each other and fall in love, rather than love at first sight and it worked for me.<br><br>Beautifully written, I cannot wait to read the rest of the Wallflower books (disclaimer I’ve read Devil in Winter and Again the Magic, but I still really want to read the other two books). This book was exactly what I needed to read at exactly the right time.<br><br><b> <i> “I'm coming to believe that there are two kinds of people... those who choose to be masters of their own fate and those who wait in chairs while other dance. I would rather be one of the former than the latter.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13443455824787306861"><b>Finally, FINALLY, a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/27847.Lisa_Kleypas' title='Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lisa Kleypas</a> book that I actually <i>like</i>! I'm not broken after all!</b><br/><br/>I was beginning to think that perhaps I was the only person on earth to <i>hate</i> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/27847.Lisa_Kleypas' title='Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lisa Kleypas</a>. I 2-starred both <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/161910.Suddenly_You' title='Suddenly You by Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Suddenly You</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114173.Somewhere_I_ll_Find_You__Capital_Theatre___1_' title='Somewhere I'll Find You (Capital Theatre, #1) by Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Somewhere I'll Find You</a>, and I was really ready to just throw in the towel.   <span id="freeText13443455824787306861" style="display:none"><b>Finally, FINALLY, a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/27847.Lisa_Kleypas" title="Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Lisa Kleypas</a> book that I actually <i>like</i>! I 2-starred both <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/161910.Suddenly_You" title="Suddenly You by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Suddenly You</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114173.Somewhere_I_ll_Find_You__Capital_Theatre___1_" title="Somewhere I'll Find You (Capital Theatre, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Somewhere I'll Find You</a>, and I was really ready to just throw in the towel. However, I already owned <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114162.Secrets_of_a_Summer_Night__Wallflowers___1_" title="Secrets of a Summer Night (Wallflowers, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Secrets of a Summer Night</a> so I figured I would try <i>one</i> more time. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465272761i/19332278._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>#bathtubbook<br><br>And I'm soooo happy that I gave this one a try. <br><br>This was a great story with a complex H and h, a great set of side characters, and a romance that developed slowly over time. Despite some awkwardness between the two MCs at the 80% mark or so, the romance was simply divine. <br><br>I think I found the first Kleypas series I can get behind. Here's to hoping the rest of the books in the series will be winners too. <br><br></span>

<div id="review_797536174" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/797536174" />
    <a title="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19958389-christina-brunette-reader"><img alt="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532563583p2/19958389.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/797536174?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" href="/user/show/19958389-christina-brunette-reader">Christina ~ Brunette Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780060091293" href="/book/show/774635.Secrets_of_a_Summer_Night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19958389-christina-brunette-reader?shelf=historical-romance-victorian">historical-romance-victorian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19958389-christina-brunette-reader?shelf=victorian-early-1837-1850">victorian-early-1837-1850</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer797536174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15589670697523203050">Finally getting around this vintage Kleypas. I found it much better written and engaging than her latest historical offerings, which I recently read, though I must also admit I enjoyed <i>Secrets of a Summer Night</i> more as a fun series set-up than for the romance itself.<br/><br/>Long story short, Annabelle Payton is a genteel but destitute beauty who needs to marry for money, quickly. Simon Hunt wants her, he's handsome and now filthy rich, and well-connected into the Ton, but remains a cleaned-up butcher's </span>
  <span id="freeText15589670697523203050" style="display:none">Finally getting around this vintage Kleypas. I found it much better written and engaging than her latest historical offerings, which I recently read, though I must also admit I enjoyed <i>Secrets of a Summer Night</i> more as a fun series set-up than for the romance itself.<br /><br />Long story short, Annabelle Payton is a genteel but destitute beauty who needs to marry for money, quickly. Simon Hunt wants her, he's handsome and now filthy rich, and well-connected into the Ton, but remains a cleaned-up butcher's son, therefore he won't do. No, no and no! *stomps dainty foot*<br /><br />Oh, conflicts that shouldn't be conflicts, how many innumerable romance books have they spawned?<br /><br />She must be a manipulative uppity lightskirt because... she just is and is been giving me the cold-shoulder for the last couple of Seasons!! He must be a selfish, unsuitable boor because... reasons!!<br />Let's see how long it takes her to become desperate enough to accept a "would you be my mistress" proposition. Let's see if I can be the Self-Victimising Queen of the year (1843, by the way).<br /><br />A little more pragmatism from the heroine's part and a little less cynicism from the hero's and this book would have ended by what, page 50? I understand the need of a plot, and this type of scenario can be a legitimate one as any, but at the same time I've never been fond of storylines where each lead is ready to uncritically assume the worst about the other almost at first sight, so it was hard for me to warm up to both Annabelle and Simon. They eventually come to their senses pretty soon, it's a romance after all, though despite the unconvincing villain sub-thread kicking in to infuse some action, the gist of things seemed to boil down to the basic fact that the heroine had to reconsider her morals and overcome her snobbery about the hero's origins. Meh.<br /><br />That said, this is still a quite satisfying read, just not as outstanding as I was hoping for. The writing flowed, there were some nice touches of humour and Kleypas's ability to convey the couple's chemistry and sensuality always top rate, if here somehow disjointed from the emotional progression. <br />The best parts were the scenes involving the secondary characters and their relationship with the protagonists and reading about how the four Wallflowers meet and become a team was really enjoyable. Same goes for Simon's interactions with two future heroes, which also give deeper background information on the "world" the author has created for this series and which sound like very promising material for the following books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15589670697523203050" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

That should be interesting. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488716722i/22147165._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer49907675" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9215304338883774862"><i>Re-read 10/8/19</i><br/><br/><i>Original read/review Jan'2010</i>:<br/><br/>5+ stars – Historical Romance<br/><br/>This is a great start to a fun, dazzlingly romantic series about four young ladies with very different personalities and backgrounds entering society who form a deep bond of friendship that grounds them as they traverse the rocky course of relationships and husband hunting in stuffy Victorian era England.<br/><br/>Beautiful Annabelle Peyton is determined to find a wealthy suitor with a high position in society to wed in order to sav</span>
  <span id="freeText9215304338883774862" style="display:none"><i>Re-read 10/8/19</i><br /><br /><i>Original read/review Jan'2010</i>:<br /><br />5+ stars – Historical Romance<br /><br />This is a great start to a fun, dazzlingly romantic series about four young ladies with very different personalities and backgrounds entering society who form a deep bond of friendship that grounds them as they traverse the rocky course of relationships and husband hunting in stuffy Victorian era England.<br /><br />Beautiful Annabelle Peyton is determined to find a wealthy suitor with a high position in society to wed in order to save her family from financial ruin. Simon Hunt is a commoner with a self-made empire of vast wealth and power who infuriates and tempts her at every turn. He makes it clear that although he wants to be the one to introduce Annabelle to the wonders of passion, he won’t offer her marriage. Of course, it doesn’t take long before he falls hard for Annabelle, but can Simon and her friends, the wallflowers, convince her to take a chance on a love match?<br /> <br />Simon is such a butter-melting, swoon-worthy, amazing, romantic, and devoted hero...just yum! It’s a wonderful start to a truly amazing series! Big 5 stars!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300524675" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer742956338612946018">I've put off reading this series for so long and I have no idea why! I read the Hathaway books and thought nothing in the HR world could compare. Was I being a tad too judgmental? Maybe. Am I questioning my fierce love of the Hathaway clan? Hell no! Cam's a delicious bit of man and remains to this day one of my favorite book boyfriends.<br/><br/>That being said, I'm adding Simon Hunt to that list. Tall, dark, brooding and "commanding" in certain areas of his life <i>*ahem*</i>. Oh hell yes! Annabelle was a fanta</span>
  <span id="freeText742956338612946018" style="display:none">I've put off reading this series for so long and I have no idea why! I read the Hathaway books and thought nothing in the HR world could compare. Was I being a tad too judgmental? Maybe. Am I questioning my fierce love of the Hathaway clan? Hell no! Cam's a delicious bit of man and remains to this day one of my favorite book boyfriends.<br /><br />That being said, I'm adding Simon Hunt to that list. Tall, dark, brooding and "commanding" in certain areas of his life <i>*ahem*</i>. Oh hell yes! Annabelle was a fantastic match for him and I loved the give and take of their relationship until they finally both (thank you, baby Jesus!) gave in and experienced the wonderful. <br /><br />Well done again, Ms. Kleypas. I look forward to reading the rest of this series.</span>

<div id="review_1048504716" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1048504716" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1048504716?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/22068159-secrets-of-a-summer-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=series-standalone-stories">series-standalone-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-historical">romance-m-f-historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-audio">romance-m-f-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1048504716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16195823745511645026"><i>Written April 5, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>4 Stars - Charming, steamy and much chuckling fun. These determined 'Wallflowers' are women to admire</b><br/><br/>Yet another amusing <i>'Wallflowers'</i> HR as audiobook (11 hrs) narrated by always excellent <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/474459.Rosalyn_Landor' title='Rosalyn Landor' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rosalyn Landor</a>. (You get this one for just $7 incl. the e-book / kindle at Amazon right now.) <br/><br/><a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/6e860d2b-4edf-4212-a78c-511350cc04e7_zpspefkcesz.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428245422i/14394180.jpg' alt=' photo 6e860d2b-4edf-4212-a78c-511350cc04e7_zpspefkcesz.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Well done, well narrated, very entertaining HR</b><br/>I liked the of many readers so much beloved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114166.Devil_in_Winter__Wallflowers___3_' title='Devil in Winter (Wallflowers, #3) by Lisa Kleypas' rel='nofollow noopener'>Devil in Winter</a> (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1048499389?<br%20/>book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>#3 - 3.9 stars</a>) some weeks ago and this series instalment was just as well written, f</span>
  <span id="freeText16195823745511645026" style="display:none"><i>Written April 5, 2015</i><br><br><b>4 Stars - Charming, steamy and much chuckling fun. These determined 'Wallflowers' are women to admire</b><br><br>Yet another amusing <i>'Wallflowers'</i> HR as audiobook (11 hrs) narrated by always excellent <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/474459.Rosalyn_Landor" title="Rosalyn Landor" rel="nofollow noopener">Rosalyn Landor</a>. (You get this one for just $7 incl. the e-book / kindle at Amazon right now.) <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/6e860d2b-4edf-4212-a78c-511350cc04e7_zpspefkcesz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428245422i/14394180.jpg" alt=" photo 6e860d2b-4edf-4212-a78c-511350cc04e7_zpspefkcesz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Well done, well narrated, very entertaining HR</b><br>I liked the of many readers so much beloved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114166.Devil_in_Winter__Wallflowers___3_" title="Devil in Winter (Wallflowers, #3) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">Devil in Winter</a> (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1048499389?&lt;br%20/&gt;book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">#3 - 3.9 stars</a>) some weeks ago and this series instalment was just as well written, funny and filled with interesting characters. Looking forward to read about the American sisters and their way to love soon too. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><i>London, 1843</i><br><br><i>Secrets of a Summer Night</i> is the first 'Wallflowers' part and it is about the beautiful <b>Annabelle Peyton</b>. A 25 years old woman in a urgent need of a (rich) suitable husband. She has tried in several seasons to find a match to 'save' her mother and younger brother. But without wealth, assets, other than a pretty face, in her bride coffin it is quite hopeless.<br><br><b>Mr. Simon Hunt</b> is a new player in the ballrooms that has an "good eye" (an lust..) for Annabelle. Once was Simon just the local butcher’s son but is by now both very wealthy and powerful. Nevertheless maybe not the "right" kind of admirer for a well born young lady like Annabelle. In her opinion anyway. <br><blockquote>‘What was she doing? Continuing this game, maintaining even this fragile communication with him, was pointless. No …it was dangerous. There was no choice to be made between safety and disaster.’</blockquote><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>What I maybe like most about this book is that our heroine here isn't</b> always a good &amp; nice girl. Annabelle is both pretty self-absorbed and indeed selfish. Well not always, sure she cares about her mother, brother and girlfriends (these interesting three other Wallflowers) but she also has some narrow-minded preconceptions, she often look down on others and are incredibly snobby when it comes to social class and the nobility. Though it's fun, I actually like the privilege to avoid having to face another admirable good-hearted young historical heroine occasionally. <br><br>Thus said, so fits course this little rougher, harder and cynical "working class" hero, Simon Hunt, her perfectly. They are like two confused magnets that lost each other and yet still not understood it.<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/857d0796edeca1fad1fb490bc9c9c472_zps1c87c057.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428214627i/14389230.jpg" alt=" photo 857d0796edeca1fad1fb490bc9c9c472_zps1c87c057.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br> .. <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Cartoon/Couple%20drawings/76a79466-11ab-462e-8650-7d17038b9d42_zpslvbqctsu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428179254i/14382757.jpg" alt=" photo 76a79466-11ab-462e-8650-7d17038b9d42_zpslvbqctsu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘Annabelle could hardly fail to note the differences between them. Hunt looked positively swarthy in the gathering dusk, big and potently masculine, with the eyes of a pirate and the casually ruthless air of a pagan king. He was no less arrogant than he had ever been…no tamer, no more refined…and yet somehow he had become the object of such all- consuming desire that Annabelle was certain she had lost her mind.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/857d0796edeca1fad1fb490bc9c9c472_zps1c87c057.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428214627i/14389230.jpg" alt=" photo 857d0796edeca1fad1fb490bc9c9c472_zps1c87c057.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>Was it really that bad back in 1840s?</b><br>Another common beliefs in this particular historical, that really surprises me, is that the men here seem to think it is completely cool to wait out attractive women as 'poor' Annabelle until they were irremediable spinsters. Then they could be bought cheaply as dependent mistresses (sex-slaves) at a more convenient way than as spouses. The strong <i>women's rights</i> part in me wanted to scream and yell. ~ Ugh, for cold-hearted self-righteous men. <br><br><b>Thanksgod Mr Hunt was a true gentleman</b>, surprisingly but he did the 'right' thing, in the end. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br>Ms Kleypas is maybe not my absolute number #1 favorite in this HR genre but her books are nevertheless amusing and very steamy stories. There will be many more. <br><blockquote>“Having regrets is the only sign that you’ve done anything interesting with your life.”</blockquote><br><b>I LIKE - good historical romances in my headphones</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16195823745511645026" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1578257071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11626300229582634152"><b>Never has man trapping been so much fun to read</b><br/><br/>Big thanks to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alp</a> for the Buddy Read.<br/><br/><b>Setting / Time / Genre:</b> Regency, England<br/><br/><b>Length:</b> 384 pages <br/><br/><b>Series:</b> Yes and I believe but am not entirely certain I have read the other three. Re-read may be in the works. <br/><br/><b>Sexy times:</b> Light on the sexy sexerson. By my definition, that it. <br/><br/><b>Plan on reading more by the author: </b> Sure am!<br/><br/><b>Synopsis in one sentence or slightly more:</b> Annabelle's family is basically destitute and she conspires with her wallflower friends to </span>
  <span id="freeText11626300229582634152" style="display:none"><b>Never has man trapping been so much fun to read</b><br><br>Big thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a> for the Buddy Read.<br><br><b>Setting / Time / Genre:</b> Regency, England<br><br><b>Length:</b> 384 pages <br><br><b>Series:</b> Yes and I believe but am not entirely certain I have read the other three. Re-read may be in the works. <br><br><b>Sexy times:</b> Light on the sexy sexerson. By my definition, that it. <br><br><b>Plan on reading more by the author: </b> Sure am!<br><br><b>Synopsis in one sentence or slightly more:</b> Annabelle's family is basically destitute and she conspires with her wallflower friends to trap a member of the peer but instead end up with the utterly delectable Simon who is a man of trade (damn, how is that for a run on sentence?).<br><br><b>Heroine:</b> Annabelle. Ok, let us be honest. MANIPULATIVE. And I get it You are broke, dearest Annabelle. But you and your cackling group of friends, were a challenge for me to love. I mean a few of you were awesome. You were ok. Only ok. For the first half of the book. Then you rescued Simon. And you were a little more than ok. <br><br>Read the book and you will understand this part:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463931901ra/19176617.gif" width="400" height="150" alt="blown" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Hero:</b> Simon. At first, you too filled the only OK shoes. You were an ass, out to trap Miss Annabelle as your mistress. But then, you became awesome. A hero. Calm in the face of the storm. You became delicious. Read this book for Simon if nothing else. <br><br><b>Why it did or didn't work for me:</b> I do not do well reading about manipulative women. It's distasteful. Annabelle never really became a heroine I would be interested in reading about nor one I liked. Even after her rescue. I found her more than a little vapid. Nothing kills a book faster, you know? <br><br>Try Evie's book. I recall that I liked that one. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer9589081736408335723"><b>4.0 "Island of the Misfits " stars<br/><br/>What a wonderful start to the series! A group of wallflower misfits make a pact to help each other snag husbands. I love how each member has one a major flaw that makes them an unsuitable bride.<br/><br/>Annabelle</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1563470503i/27849040._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='606' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Annabelle is beautiful but dirt poor.   <span id="freeText9589081736408335723" style="display:none"><b>4.0 "Island of the Misfits " stars<br><br>What a wonderful start to the series! <div id="review_98335934" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/98335934" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/98335934?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-historical-romance">genre-historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-lisa-kleypas">author-lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-alpha">hero-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=funny-funny-har-har">funny-funny-har-har</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-hot-male-in-my-harem">hero-hot-male-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=faves-kings-of-the-harem">faves-kings-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-self-made-man">hero-self-made-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-blue-collar">hero-blue-collar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer98335934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17511856073364562840"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/02/review-secrets-of-a-summer-night-by-lisa-kleypas.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550694r/16122391.jpg%20' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Miss Annabelle Payton, Miss Lillian Bowman, Miss Evangeline Jenner and Miss Daisy Bowman are regular sights at the peripheral of a ballroom. With each young lady having oddities and foibles that make them untenable to the bachelors of the ton. However, they strike up an unlikely friendship each vowing to help the others out to find a husband by means fair and foul. With the beautiful and spirited Annabelle being the first...<br/><br/>Miss Annabelle Payton’s family are on the knife edge of poverty, to </span>
  <span id="freeText17511856073364562840" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/02/review-secrets-of-a-summer-night-by-lisa-kleypas.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550694r/16122391.jpg%20" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Miss Annabelle Payton, Miss Lillian Bowman, Miss Evangeline Jenner and Miss Daisy Bowman are regular sights at the peripheral of a ballroom. With each young lady having oddities and foibles that make them untenable to the bachelors of the ton. However, they strike up an unlikely friendship each vowing to help the others out to find a husband by means fair and foul. With the beautiful and spirited Annabelle being the first...<br><br>Miss Annabelle Payton’s family are on the knife edge of poverty, to stop these dire straits Annabelle must marry and marry well. However, with no dowry to speak and it approaching her fourth season it is becoming nigh on impossible to catch a husband, let alone a peer of the realm. Instead she is starting to receive more dishonourable offers of becoming a mistress, offers that it seems she may have to consider if things don't change soon. One of these men is a Mr Simon Hunt, who has been longing for Annabelle for two long years, despite her repeated rebuffs, but he soon sees his opportunity when they are both invited to the country for a house party. However the Wallflowers also see the same opportunity for Annabelle to find a suitable husband. Let the games begin...<br><br>This is one of my favourite series, and Mr Simon Hunt is one of my favourite heroes. He is a self made man, a son of a butcher who has made his fortune in financial speculation and then on the blossoming trade of the railway. However, no matter how rich he is, he still will never fit in with the upper echelons of society, something that bothers him not at all. He is blunt, honest and very sure of himself (aka arrogant), how could you not love him? He also has some very dishonourable intentions toward Annabelle...to begin with, I love that as the book goes on his feelings towards Annabelle deepen; in this book it is more a case of lust at first sight rather than love. That is why I loved that Annabelle was such a strong heroine, I think if she was a weaker person and gave in to Simon at the beginning then this story would have been vastly different, and not so happily resolved. The love story between these two was very passionate and there were some hot sex scenes in the book (one in a linen closet, which is most definately my favourite!) which added nicely to the couples growing affection for each other.<br><br>I also liked the introduction to the other Wallflowers, each having their own very distinct personalities and I look forward to reading Lillian’s book next. One of my favourite parts of the book was when the girls were playing rounders-in-knickers, it was a very funny scene that never fails to have me in fits of giggles.<br><br>This book is very polished and well written, especially the dialogue, the interactions between the characters are really good, sometimes funny, sometimes intense and other times romantic. The conversations and banter between the wallflowers especially Lillian and Daisy Bowman shows their relationship of teasing and close sisters perfectly, and the conversations between Annabelle and Simon are equally sharp and witty. As well as this the language is elegant and seems very much in keeping with the language of the day, this isn’t a contemporary book dressed in a historical setting. LK gets her setting very well with enough detail to keep it interesting but not bogging you down in details about that historical period.<br><br>I have read this book many times and it is one of my favourite series a must read for those who love romance, especially Historical Romance. ﻿<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456260703i/18211782.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17511856073364562840" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_146690490" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/146690490" />
    <a title="Ronyell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell"><img alt="Ronyell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506581787p2/1169488.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/146690490?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronyell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronyell" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell">Ronyell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lisa Kleypas Fans!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=english-books">english-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=lisa-kleypas">lisa-kleypas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=my-blog-reviews">my-blog-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=sexy-good-girl-heroine">sexy-good-girl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=adult-book">adult-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=british-hero-or-heroine">british-hero-or-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=ronyell-s-epinions-reviews">ronyell-s-epinions-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146690490" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2844681889416210300">Why is it every time that I read a book by Lisa Kleypas, I am always so into the characters and the situations that surrounds them? Well, the answer to that is that Lisa Kleypas is clearly a brilliant romance writer and reading many of her books has been an awesome experience that I have enjoyed doing over and over again! This time, I have read the first book in Lisa Kleypas’ “Wallflower” series called “Secrets of a Summer Night” and it is surely full of drama, thrills and hot romance that will </span>
  <span id="freeText2844681889416210300" style="display:none">Why is it every time that I read a book by Lisa Kleypas, I am always so into the characters and the situations that surrounds them? Well, the answer to that is that Lisa Kleypas is clearly a brilliant romance writer and reading many of her books has been an awesome experience that I have enjoyed doing over and over again! This time, I have read the first book in Lisa Kleypas’ “Wallflower” series called “Secrets of a Summer Night” and it is surely full of drama, thrills and hot romance that will surely put any romance fan in a soothing mood!<br /><br />Annabelle Peyton, well known for being a wallflower in London society, vows to seek a worthy husband to cover her family’s debt since she does not have a dowry that would make her worthy in any nobleman’s eyes. However, Annabelle has her sights set on Lord Kendall, a lord who is currently unmarried, but suddenly, Annabelle realizes that Simon Hunt, a mysterious man that Annabelle met years ago, is also after her heart and plans to make Annabelle his alone! Will Annabelle allow Simon into her life? Read this book to find out!<br /><br />Oh my goodness! Words cannot describe how much I loved this book from Lisa Kleypas’ popular “Wallflower” series! Lisa Kleypas has done an excellent job at writing this romantic tale of what true love is all about! What I really loved about this book were the characters themselves, especially Annabelle Peyton and Simon Hunt as they are both strong and interesting characters! Let me start with Simon Hunt first since I am really interested in his character. Simon Hunt is easily one of the best romance heroes ever created because not only does he have an awesome muscular body that makes him somewhat of a superhuman, but he has a heart full of gold as he deeply cares for Annabelle during her time of need and he is willing to put his life in the line if anything happens to Annabelle and it was that personality trait of Simon’s that made me really love his character. I have briefly mentioned about Simon’s muscular body and I just love any romance hero who has muscles of steel, especially in the case of Simon as Lisa Kleypas makes sure that the audience knows how hard Simon’s muscles are! Another character I really loved in this book was Annabelle Peyton herself as she is clearly a strong and independent woman who does not let anyone get in the way of her goal of obtaining a husband. I will admit at first that I got a little annoyed with Annabelle always dismissing Simon, even though it is clear from the get go that Simon is a seriously pleasant man, but once she found out what a gentle and loyal man Simon is, she cared as much for Simon as Simon did for her and I was just so amazed at the lengths that Annabelle took to protect Simon! I also loved the brief little relationship between Lord Westcliff and Lillian Bowman as they clearly hate each other, but I guess once I read the rest of the “Wallflower” series, they might change their tune. And let us not forget about the sizzling love making scenes between Annabelle and Simon as they are extremely out of this world hot and they provide the best love making dialogues I have ever read from any romance novel like:<br /><br /><i>“I want to make you scream and claw and faint in my arms.”</i><br /><br />For anyone who do not like reading about sex scenes in a book, this book has many sex scenes between Annabelle and Simon and it would be best to skip over these scenes if they are uncomfortable to read through.<br /><br />Overall, “Secrets of a Summer Night” is a clearly extraordinary book from the great romantic mind of Lisa Kleypas that all romance novel fans will enjoy for many years to come!<br /><br /><b>Review is also on: <a href="http://rabbitearsbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/03/secrets-of-summer-night-by-lisa-kleypas.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabbit Ears Book Blog</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2844681889416210300" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
