<span id="freeTextContainer17921224593083089839"><br/><b> My Review::</b><br/><br/>This was a very easy, enjoyable read and though it seemed to drag in the beginning, I did learn things about class distinction that I had not been aware of.<br/><br/>I am adding Simon Hunt to my rapidly growing list of favorite heroes, but I can't tell you how many times I wanted to kick Annabelle to the curb. Hmmm...did they have curbs back then? Well, if the did she would have found herself sitting on one had I had my way.<br/><br/>I enjoyed the devious banter between the wallflowers, Annabelle, Lilli</span>
  <span id="freeText17921224593083089839" style="display:none"><br /><b> My Review::</b><br /><br />This was a very easy, enjoyable read and though it seemed to drag in the beginning, I did learn things about class distinction that I had not been aware of.<br /><br />I am adding Simon Hunt to my rapidly growing list of favorite heroes, but I can't tell you how many times I wanted to kick Annabelle to the curb. Hmmm...did they have curbs back then? Well, if the did she would have found herself sitting on one had I had my way.<br /><br />I enjoyed the devious banter between the wallflowers, Annabelle, Lillian, Evie and Daisy. I thought they balanced each other nicely. I loved that they were not willing to sit idly by while life moved on without them, and their witty insights and plottings made this a fun read.<br /><br />Simon Hunt should be given Sainthood for the amount of patience he showed while waiting for Annabelle to come to her senses and realize that he wasn't the bottom of the barrel. I was a tad disappointed in him and his readiness to make her into his mistress rather than make a marriage proposal, but hey, it all worked out in the end which is where it matters most.<br /><br />I'm moving forward with It Happened One Autumn and can't wait to see Lillian and Marcus drive themselves insane with their attempts to annoy one another.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17921224593083089839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

I don't particularly enjoy seeing the class distinction and resulting snobbery. <br/><br/>I will definitely be listening to the rest of the series in the future.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11124263101563416325"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1557926903i/27512679._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every time I see you,” he murmured, “I think you couldn’t possibly become any more beautiful—and you always prove me wrong.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>What a journey this was. I honestly did not like these characters in the beginning of the book. That is to say, I didn't like the heroine. At all. And I had trouble understanding the hero's interest in her. She was shallow and self-serving, just as Lord Westcliff had described her. But after a rather significant turning point in the story, and in her cha</span>
  <span id="freeText11124263101563416325" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1557926903i/27512679._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every time I see you,” he murmured, “I think you couldn’t possibly become any more beautiful—and you always prove me wrong.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>What a journey this was. I honestly did not like these characters in the beginning of the book. That is to say, I didn't like the heroine. At all. And I had trouble understanding the hero's interest in her. She was shallow and self-serving, just as Lord Westcliff had described her. But after a rather significant turning point in the story, and in her character, I ended up rather LOVING them both. It was kind of like watching someone grow up right before your eyes. And Simon... oh Simon was just fucking perfect. I ADORE HIM! <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Kiss me again.” “No, I’ll hurt you. I’m leaning on your leg.” “That’s not my leg,” came his roguish reply, making her laugh. “You perverse man.” “You’re so beautiful,” Simon whispered. “Inside and out. Annabelle, my wife, my sweet love…kiss me again. And don’t stop until I tell you to.” “Yes, Simon,” she murmured, and cheerfully obeyed.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I do believe he might make my list of all-time favorite heroes. (come to think of it, that list is getting pretty lengthy.). Full marks, Ms. Kleypas, although I still haven't figured out where the title came from. 🤔</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" href="/user/show/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus">Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=scribd">scribd</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=historical">historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2886626255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer508638203538879170"><b>Audio: 4 STARS!<br/>Story: 3.75 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I hate everything that keeps you separate from me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>While it wasn't the best Lisa Kleypas I've ever read, <i>Secrets of a Summer Night</i> was definitely worth reading. Annabelle and Simon were lots of fun. And I loved the Wallflowers themselves.<br/><br/>One thing I have to give LK props for is pulling off a story where the H has questionable motives (which is especially difficult in a historical setting, imo, since men are supposed to have honor.) But here, I liked</span>
  <span id="freeText508638203538879170" style="display:none"><b>Audio: 4 STARS!<br />Story: 3.75 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I hate everything that keeps you separate from me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>While it wasn't the best Lisa Kleypas I've ever read, <i>Secrets of a Summer Night</i> was definitely worth reading. Annabelle and Simon were lots of fun. And I loved the Wallflowers themselves.<br /><br />One thing I have to give LK props for is pulling off a story where the H has questionable motives (which is especially difficult in a historical setting, imo, since men are supposed to have honor.) But here, I liked the evolution of Simon's desire to make Annabelle his mistress; their journey from enemies to lovers/spouses was wholly believable and enjoyable.<br /><br />However, what almost ruined this book for me was that ridiculously OTT ending sequence that came out of nowhere in the last 10%. What the heck was that?<br /><br />Anyway, I've already started book 2....so far Lillian has shown herself to be a heroine after my own heart, lol.</span>

<div id="review_2461234208" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2461234208" />
    <a title="Curlyhairlass19" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66567617-curlyhairlass19"><img alt="Curlyhairlass19" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554498726p2/66567617.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2461234208?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Curlyhairlass19" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Curlyhairlass19" href="/user/show/66567617-curlyhairlass19">Curlyhairlass19</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2461234208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15870465127015256297">5 stars for Annabelle & Simon Hunt’s story!! I literally could not put this one down. I love the banter back and forth, the obvious intrigue, and sexual tension. Annabelle, willing to be a mistress just so she can save her family. This was somewhat of a enemies to lovers type trope, but not entirely. <br/><br/>I love how they chose to love each other, and didn’t fully realize it at first. This book was packed with so much! Humor, angst, steaminess etc.. I feel like I’m fumbling in the dark for words, but </span>
  <span id="freeText15870465127015256297" style="display:none">5 stars for Annabelle &amp; Simon Hunt’s story!! I literally could not put this one down. I love the banter back and forth, the obvious intrigue, and sexual tension. Annabelle, willing to be a mistress just so she can save her family. This was somewhat of a enemies to lovers type trope, but not entirely. <br /><br />I love how they chose to love each other, and didn’t fully realize it at first. This book was packed with so much! Humor, angst, steaminess etc.. I feel like I’m fumbling in the dark for words, but all I know is that I LOVED this book hard!<br /><br />“Let me take care of you. You’ve never had anyone to lean on, have you? I’ve got strong shoulders, Annabelle.” A deep laugh rumbled in his chest. “And I may possibly be the only man of your acquaintance who’ll be able to afford you.”<br /><br />“Why offer to marry me when you might have me as your mistress?” He nuzzled her throat gently. “Because I realized during the past few days that I can’t leave doubt in anyone’s mind about to whom you belong. Especially not yours.”<br /><br />Friendship came first. Love came when they least expected it. I loved how this book didn’t have the assumed HEA that you might think. I really enjoy books that allow us to see how a couple deals with married life, and how the choosing to love deepens. Love is a choice, you don’t just fall into it.</span>

<div id="review_886370487" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/886370487" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/886370487?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=v-card">v-card</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer886370487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8336784309500797870"><b>4.5 This series is fantastic!!!</b><br/><br/>I’ve been sick for the past few days and what I really wanted were some good romance books to comfort me. Some people eat chicken soup, I curl up with Lisa Kleypas, who I think is one of the best historical romance writers.<br/><br/>If you haven’t read this series, you really need to. The series is about 4 ladies and they are consider Wallflowers, which basically means they aren’t the traditional English single ladies and because they are so very untraditional, they aren’t d</span>
  <span id="freeText8336784309500797870" style="display:none"><b>4.5 This series is fantastic!!!</b><br /><br />I’ve been sick for the past few days and what I really wanted were some good romance books to comfort me. Some people eat chicken soup, I curl up with Lisa Kleypas, who I think is one of the best historical romance writers.<br /><br />If you haven’t read this series, you really need to. The series is about 4 ladies and they are consider Wallflowers, which basically means they aren’t the traditional English single ladies and because they are so very untraditional, they aren’t desirable.<br /><br />The first book is Annabelle’s book. She’s poor with no dowry. The only thing she can offer is a title, but even then no one wants to marry a girl with no dowry, even if she is very very very pretty.<br /><br />I wasn’t sure I was going to like Annabelle. I found her very selfish, conceited and very snobby. But I do like that she was pushed down a peg or two because she’s a very snobby poor girl.<br /><br />Annabelle and Simon met one night and had one kiss. It’s two years later and Annabelle is still single and looking for a husband. This is the last season for her to find a husband before she is considered a spinster and no one will want her. Her option is to becomes someone mistress or marry a poor English gentleman.<br /><br />So Annabelle is desperate, you would think she wouldn’t be so choosy, considering the RICH Simon Hunt is well on the hunt for her, but no, she is picky because Simon doesn’t have a title! Heaven forbid she marries a man without a title, even though he’s MEGA rich. It was really hard for me to grasp this concept, but Lisa does a very good job in explaining how hard it would be for a traditional title girl to marry below her class.<br /><br />The whole book is about Simon hunting for Annabelle and I LOVED IT! I love it when the hero chases after the Heroine. I love the banter between the main characters and I couldn’t get enough of it. I just love being sucked in this world and I never wanted it to end! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8336784309500797870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9gdmG71/WIilrpaCDyTJtFZ/60iychndnUUbxA6lkafCkXT4CynND9bfu9rTHmPlOd0X488a+jlX+HmJn9jFtQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1UDwCxF1S0doF6jZCSI6Nqjefpz8+/vaUmh4P7Kbyfbh1uLopyPewBtmhYHVGJBnx3yCN4GTGD6Y1RpyI+ad5A==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/760678-secrets-of-a-summer-night">Quotes from Secrets of a Summ...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Having regrets is the only sign that you’ve done anything interesting with your life.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/348160-having-regrets-is-the-only-sign-that-you-ve-done-anything">160 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>

          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Annabelle’s eyes stung as she stared at him, while need and inexhaustible tenderness gathered like an ache in her body. “I realized something,” she said huskily, “when I was standing outside the foundry, watching it burn and knowing you were inside.” She swallowed hard against the thickness in her throat. “I would rather have died in your arms, Simon, than face a lifetime without you. All those endless years… all those winters, summers… a hundred seasons of wanting you and never having you. Growing old, while you stayed eternally young in my memories.” She bit her lip and shook her head, while her eyes flooded. “I was wrong when I told you that I didn’t know where I belonged. I do. With you, Simon. Nothing matters except being with you. You’re stuck with me forever, and I’ll never listen when you tell me to go.” She managed a tremulous smile. “So you may as well stop complaining and resign yourself to it.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
